//　５年目のオヤシロさまの祟りは、......沙都子の叔父が死に、俺が消えたこと＠
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLineAll("", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }

		   NULL, "Oyashiro-sama's curse on the fifth year... was Satoko's uncle dying and me disappearing.", GetGlobalFlag(GLinemodeSp));

	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLineAll("", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	OutputLine(NULL, "　仲間たちは俺の失踪を嘆きながらも…たくましく立ち直ろうとしているかもしれない。",
		   NULL, "Maybe my friends were all lamenting my disappearance... and valiantly trying to get back on their feet.", GetGlobalFlag(GLinemodeSp));
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { ClearMessage(); } else { OutputLineAll(NULL, "\n\n", Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }

//　.........そして...４人になってしまったけれども、......部活を再開して...４人で賑やかにやっているのだ＠
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLineAll("", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	OutputLine(NULL, "　………そして…４人になってしまったけれども、……部活を再開して…４人で賑やかにやっているのだ。",
		   NULL, "...And... even though they were down to four people... the club would re-open... and they would have a good time without me.", GetGlobalFlag(GLinemodeSp));
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { ClearMessage(); } else { OutputLineAll(NULL, "\n\n", Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }

//　.........いつの日にか、...俺が帰ってくるのを待ちながら￥
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLineAll("", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	OutputLine(NULL, "　………いつの日にか、…俺が帰ってくるのを待ちながら。",
		   NULL, "...Waiting... for the day when I would come back.", Line_Normal);

//　ごめん、みんな＠........................俺、!w1000...帰れなかった￥
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLineAll("", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	OutputLine(NULL, "　ごめん、みんな。",
		   NULL, "I'm sorry, everyone.", Line_WaitForInput);

		   NULL, " ............I...", Line_ContinueAfterTyping);

		   NULL, " couldn't come back home.", Line_Normal);

	OutputLine(NULL, "　沙都子の笑顔を願う、にーにーとしての勤めだった。",
		   NULL, "It was my wish for Satoko's smile—and my duty as her Nii-nii.", GetGlobalFlag(GLinemodeSp));
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { ClearMessage(); } else { OutputLineAll(NULL, "\n", Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }


//　もうこれで、...お前をいじめるヤツはこの世にひとりも残っていない＠
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLineAll("", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	OutputLine(NULL, "　もうこれで、…お前をいじめるヤツはこの世にひとりも残っていない。",

	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { ClearMessage(); } else { OutputLineAll(NULL, "\n\n", Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }

//　...俺と悟史の、二人のにーにーが二年かけて成し遂げたから￥

	OutputLine(NULL, "　…俺と悟史の、二人のにーにーが二年かけて成し遂げたから。",
		   NULL, "...Because Satoshi and I... it took two years, but we succeeded.", Line_Normal);
	ClearMessage();

//　お前の小憎らしい、八重歯の似合う笑顔...＠.........もう一度、!w1000......見たかった￥

		   NULL, "That annoying, toothy smile of yours...", Line_WaitForInput);

		   NULL, " We wanted to see it...", Line_ContinueAfterTyping);

	SetValidityOfInput( FALSE );
	Wait( 1000 );
	SetValidityOfInput( TRUE );

	OutputLine(NULL, "……見たかった。",
		   NULL, " one more time.", Line_Normal);
	ClearMessage();
	DisableWindow();
